 aaj swami vivekanand kii anany sahyogi or shishy bhagini nivedita kaa janmdin he
 His original name was Margaret Elizabeth Noble
 vah irish mul kii thim
 Come learn about Sister Nivedita
 1
 Margaret alias Bhagini Nivedita, who played an active role in the movement for women's education and independence, was born on 28 October 1867 in County Tyrone, Ireland
 2
 His father, Samuel Richmond Noble, was a pastor and taught his daughter human service
 3
 When Nivedita was just 10 years old, her father died
 unka paalan-poshan naanaa hamiltan ne kiya
 4
 nivedita kii shuruaati padhai ke dauraan kala or sangeet main dilchaspee thi
 When he grew up, he decided to work as a teacher
 5
 He completed his education from Halifax College
 unhone bhautikee, kala, sangeet, sahitya samet kai vishyon kaa gahan adhyayan kiya
 She was 17 years old when she became a teacher
 6
 1895 marked a turning point in his life
 is saal landan main unki swami vivekanand se mulaakaat hui
 She was so impressed with Swamiji that after three years she came to make India her work place
 7
 Margaret had some doubts and uncertainties about the fundamental ideas of religion at a young age, for which she met Swami Vivekananda through an acquaintance of her, Lady Margessan
 8
 Swami Vivekananda initiated Noble as a disciple on 25 March 1898
 vivekanand ne unase bhagwaan buddha ke karunaa ke path par chalane ko kaha
 Swami said, follow the great person who was born 500 times and devoted his life for the welfare of the people and then attained enlightenment
 9
 After initiation, Swami Vivekananda gave him the new name Nivedita
 baad main unke naam ke aage 'sistar' kaa sanskrit shabd bhagini bhi jud gaya
 10
 swami vivekanand ne margrat elizabeth nobel ko bhagini nivedita yani `ishwar ko samarpit' naam diya
 One meaning of Nivedita is also dedicated to women's education
 11
 Bhagini Nivedita wandered across India with her guru Swami Vivekananda for some time
 phir vah kalakatta (ab kolkata) main bas gayi
 12
 apane guru kii prerana se unhone kalakatta main ladakiyon ke liye skool kholaa

 13
 In contact with Bhagini Nivedita were people like Rabindranath Tagore, Jagdish Chandra Basu, Avanindranath Thakur and Nandlal Bose
 unhone rameshchandra dutt or yadunath sarkaar ko bhartiya nazariye se itihaas likhane kii prerana di
 14
 shuruyaat main nivedita maanati thim ki bharat or britain ko saath kaam karnaa chahie
 But when she saw the terrorist form of the British Raj in India, she became a victim of the freedom movement of Indians

 isliye kyonki america ne iran se niryaat par lagaae gaye apane pratibandhon se bharat sahit aath deshon ko di gai chhot jari rakhane se inkaar kar diya tha (may, 2018 main iran parmaanu samjhaute se baahar aane ke baad america ne iran or uske saath vyapaar jari rakhane vaale deshon par kadi paabandiyaan laga di thim)

5 million US dollars

 pradosh vrath main bhagavanshivaki upasna kii jaati he
 This fast is one of the most auspicious and important fasts of Hinduism
 hindu chandra calendar ke anusaarapradosh vrathchandra maas ke 13 wein din (trayodashi) par rakhaa jaataa he
 It is believed that by worshiping Lord Shiva on the day of Pradosh one gets freedom from sins and attains salvation
 is baar pradosh vrath 6 oktober yani aaj he
 According to the scriptures of Pradosha fast, keeping Pradosha fast gives the same fruits as donating two cows
 pradosh vrath ko lekar ek puranic tathy saamne aata he ki 'ek din jab chaaron or adharm kii sthiti hogi, anyaay or anachar kaa ekadhikaar hoga, manushya main swaarth bhav adhik hogi
 The person will do more at the place of performing the sinful act
 us samay main jo vyaktitrayodashika vrath rakh, shiv aradhana karegaa, us par shiv krupa hogi
 The person observing this fast goes out of the cycle of birth after birth and moves on to the path of salvation
 use utam lok kii prapti hoti he

 - nityakarmon se nivruth hokar, bhagwaan shri bhole nath kaa samaran karen
 - Diet is not taken in this fast

 - After purifying the place of worship with Ganga water or clean water, the pavilion is prepared by leaping from cow dung
 - ab is mandap main paanch rangon kaa upyog karte hue rangoli banaai jaati he

 - is prakaar pujan kii taiyaariyaan karke uttar-purvadishaki ore mukh karke baithe or bhagwaan shankar kaa pujan karnaa chahie
